 amritsar sthit swarna mandir ke paas apane hathiyaarband saathiyon ke ghere main chhipe baithe bhindrawaale or uski choti-si tukdi ko kaabo karne ke liye sena ne abhiyaan chalaaya tha
 Here are 5 major facts related to this operation
 1
 Operation Bluestar was earlier named Operation Sundown
 oparation ko yah naam isliye diya gaya ki sari karrwai aadhi raat ke baad honi thi
 Operation Sundown was actually a swoop
 iske tahat helicopter main savaar commando swarna mandir ke paas guru nanak nivas guest house main utarate or bhindrawaale ko uthaa lete
 But when Indira Gandhi did not get any satisfactory answer about the loss related to the public in this operation, this operation was put on hold
 2
 RAW had planned Operation sundown together with Mossad and it was kept secret, as India did not have diplomatic relations with Israel at the time and did not want to offend its Arab friends
 tedhvive ke paas sthit is adde par in sainik adhikariyon ko sadakon, imaaraton or gadiyon ke badi saavdhaanee se banaae gaye modelon ke bich aatank se ladane kii 22 din tak training di gai
 3

 4

 During the bloody clash between the army and the militants, Bhindranwale's military advisor Shabeg Singh wanted to fight till the sun came out so that when people came to know about the civil action, they would be killed

 World AIDS Day 2019: aids yani equared immunodefishiency syndrome ek beemaari he jo human immunodefishiency virus yaa echivi (HIV) ke kaaran hoti he
 It is a 'flu' disease soon after HIV infection

 This virus gradually reduces a person's ability to fight infection

 ' The party said it would emphasize the National Secondary Education Campaign to improve the quality of secondary education and increase resources for it and ensure enrollment of all children in secondary education in the next five years
 party ne iske alaava schuli shiksha chhodane vaale bacchon kii dar main kami laane, shiksha kaa maanakeekaran or gunvattta sunishchit karne ke liye sarkari evam nijee sansthaaon ke paryvekshan hetu swatantra niamak vyavastha sthapit karne kii bhi baat kii he
 The party in its manifesto has committed to create a national consensus on reservation for scheduled castes and scheduled tribes in the private sector
 saamaajik-aarthik evam raajnneetik parivartan ke party ke 15-sutri agenda main lacheele shram kanoon, kaale dhan ko waapas laane kii koshish or swasthya par kharch badhaakar sakal gharelu utpaada ke teen pratishat ke baraabar laane ke vaayade shaamil he
 Regarding employment generation, the manifesto said, 'within 100 days of returning to power, the party will present a broad agenda of employment to ensure that 10 crore new jobs and entrepreneurial opportunities are created for our youth
 ' It also talks about creating 60 lakh new jobs in the health sector by the year 2020, strictly enforcing all laws related to the welfare of children and further strengthening the National Child Protection Commission
 ghoshnaa patr main kaha gaya he ki kanoonee evam nyaayik sudhaar tathaa saath hi chunaav sudhaar laane ke liye nai soch evam disha apanaai jaaegi or bhrashtachar kii rokthaam se jude vidheyako ko paarit karaayaa jayega jise vipaksh ne paarit nahin hone diya he
 The manifesto states that all villages and cities will be connected to high-speed broadband connectivity within 18 months
 subah subah jab aap akhbaar main yah khabar dekhen ki 32 lakh debit card kii soochna uda lee gai he to pehle aap kya karenge? purse check karenge, card dekhenge or mobile phone main massej check karenge ki bank kii taraf se koi massej aayaa he yaa nahin
 Few people are so smart that on getting a little doubt, they immediately call customer care and block PIN numbers
 magar bahut se log aise hai jinhen pataa hi nahin chalata ki kya karen
 If someone has stolen money from a debit card or ATM card, then they do not know what the trouble is going to be about the return of that money
 baharhaal 32 lakh debit card kii jaankaree kisi ke paas chali jaae yah koi saadhaaran ghatana nahin he, iconomik times ke mutabik 32 lakh card main se 26 lakh card visa or master card hai
 6 lakh cards are mentioned on the rupay platform

 On Friday at Muktidham Ghat in Khargone city of Madhya Pradesh, a daughter lit the funeral pyre of her father and two brothers
 khargon shahar main kotwali thana antargat kaladeval maarg par tin ke bane ek makaan main karant failane se guuruuvaar ko sonu ke pita naveenchandra kasaare (50) evam do bhaaiyon jagadish (20) or kuldeep (17) kii maut ho gai thi
 Daya Patwa, the family of the deceased, told that Sonu performed the last rites at Muktidham Ghat by offering fire to the funeral pyres of these three
 unhone kaha ki isse pehle sonu ne apane pita evam do bhaaiyon kii arthi ko kandhaa diya
 People from all over the society attended this funeral
 patwa ne kaha ki sonu ke maayke main uske pita evam do bhaaiyon kii maut ke baad koi sadsy nahin bachaa tha
 So Sonu decided that she herself would offer fire to these three

 5

 The Ministry of Civil Aviation has said this
 mantralay ne yah vichaar vibhaag se sambhddha sansadeey samiti ke samaksh rakhaa he

 Rapid fluctuations in air fares have been a topic of discussion for a long time and various sections including mps have expressed concern about this and asked to make arrangements to curb price fluctuations
 samiti ko die jawaab main mantralay ne kaha ki vimaan niyam 1957 ke tahat prayek airline ko parichaalan laagat or sevaaon kii visheshtaon samet anya karkon ke aadhaar par shulk dhaancha sthapit karne kii jarurat hoti he
 It said that the government does not normally interfere in the day-to-day activities of airlines
 airlines saamaanya rup se bahut pehle tikat booking ke makasad se kam kiraaye kii peshkash karti hai
 The ministry said, "indian aviation companies operating in the Gulf regions have been asked to offer lower fares for Indian citizens
 yah kadam bhedbhavuparn yaa bazaar kharaab karne vaali keemat gatividhiyon ke daayre main aa saktaa he or videshi companiyaan isko lekar kanoonee rasta apana sakati hai
 'also, the issue of international operations by domestic airlines comes under the purview of bilateral agreements between the Government of India and foreign governments
 tippaniyan However, the Parliamentary Committee on Transport, Tourism and Culture stated that the ministry's explanation was purely technical and that it was unable to do anything under the law
 samiti ne yah sifarish kii he ki mantralay ko sabhi sambhddha pakshon se vichaar-vimarsh kar bazaar kharaab karne vaali hawaii kiraaye se nipatane ke upaay karne chahie
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) The Ministry has put this view before the Parliamentary Committee attached to the Department

 Dissatisfied with the ministry's response, the committee told the ministry that India's case should not be compared to other countries, because when a specific case occurs, a specific resolution is needed to resolve it
 hawaii kiraaye main teevr utaar-chadhaav lambey samay se charchaa kaa vishay rahaa he or saansadon samet vibhinn tabakon ne isko lekar chintaa chintaa jataai tathaa keemton main utaar-chadhaav par ankush lagane ke liye vyavastha karne ko kaha
 In its reply to the committee, the ministry said that under the Aircraft Rules 1957, each airline needs to establish a fee structure based on other factors including operating costs and characteristics of services
